Rockingham County Virginia Tombstones by Cemetery

CemeteryEast Lawn Memorial Gardens
LocationHarrisonburg, Rockingham County, Virginia. From Harrisonburg take Rt. 33 East about 2 miles. Cemetery is located on the left side of road.
NotesWell maintained. Refer to cemetery map.
Survey Date and Recorder20 Sep 2004
Martha Lee & Nettie Lee
